Please find below the test instructions (Do's & Don'ts) that is to be followed by the students during the test:

Hardware and Internet requirements:
‚Ä¢A Personal Computer / Laptop. Please don‚Äôt take the test from Mobile Browser.
‚Ä¢A Webcam connected with the System/In-built Webcam in a laptop.
‚Ä¢Smooth and uninterrupted Internet connectivity (throughout the testing session), minimum 1 MBPS/4G.	Browser/OS Requirements:
‚Ä¢This Assessment is supported by the below-listed Browsers/Versions only.
‚Ä¢Google Chrome (version 40 and above)
‚Ä¢Mozilla Firefox (version 40 and above)
‚Ä¢In case you're taking the test on Windows 8, make sure you use the latest version and disable all the popups/ notifications.
Do‚Äôs & Don‚Äôt- Instructions:
‚Ä¢Complete the test in one go, no breaks allowed in-between.
‚Ä¢This is a timed test; it is essential to keep track of time while answering the questions.
‚Ä¢Answer all the questions and complete all the modules.
‚Ä¢There is no negative marking.
‚Ä¢You cannot change your answer to any previous question.
‚Ä¢Do not click on Module Exit or Test Exit.
‚Ä¢Ensure that while taking the test, no other tab/window/link is opened simultaneously on your system else your scores will not be processed.
‚Ä¢Do not try to take screenshots of the test, else your test will be locked & you won‚Äôt be able to complete the test.
‚Ä¢Please disable all POP-UPS/ Notifications before starting the test.
‚Ä¢Ensure your face is clearly visible on the webcam. Do not wear a cap, scarf, goggles/ sunglasses, headphones, earphones, etc., or hide your face during the test.
‚Ä¢Please ensure that no one else is sitting with you during the entire duration of the test.	Steps for starting the test:
‚Ä¢For taking the exam type the URL in the address bar of the Web Browser.
‚Ä¢Enter the username and password given to you to login. Do not copy-paste the Username and Password. Always type in.
‚Ä¢Click on Start New Test.
‚Ä¢You will be automatically prompted to ‚ÄòAllow‚Äô your Camera to be enabled, please ‚ÄòACCEPT‚Äô the request. This will prompt a message ‚ÄòYou Are Under Surveillance'. Your camera is now enabled.
‚Ä¢Fill the registration form.
‚Ä¢Click on Start Test and keep a note of your AMCAT ID as mentioned on the top.
‚Ä¢To answer a question, click on Confirm and then Next to submit your answer. Do not click on Module Exit or Test Exit.
‚Ä¢If your test gets stuck at any point, there is a ‚ÄòResume Test' option that will enable you to restart the test at the same place where you got stuck. Please ensure that you Resume the Test within 2 hours of your test being stopped, otherwise your login will expire, and you won‚Äôt be able to complete the test.
 
Candidates can use our chat support with the below URL if they face any challenges during the test.
Chat Support: https://support.shl.com/categories.html?hl=en&c=10_91_12_

‚Ä¢	English (MCQ test covering Vocabulary, Grammar & Comprehension)

‚Ä¢	Quantitative Ability (MCQ test covering Basic Mathematics, Applied Mathematics, Engineering Mathematics)

‚Ä¢	Computer Science (MCQ test covering basic knowledge and understanding of computer science including concepts of operating system and computer architecture, database management and computer networks).
‚Ä¢	AUTOMATA FIX-Measures Candidate‚Äôs skill to fix faulty/incomplete source code.

24/05/25, 10:33‚ÄØpm - +91 90384 12981: *Sample HR Question:*                                                                                                                                                                               *1. Why do you want to join our company?*
Answer:
"I have researched extensively about [Company Name] and appreciate its strong reputation for innovation, professional development, and positive work culture. The company's projects align closely with my interests and skills, especially [mention specific area or project]. I see this as a great opportunity to contribute positively and grow my professional career."

*2. Why should we hire you?*
Answer:
"As a recent graduate, I bring fresh perspectives and up-to-date technical knowledge. During my B.Tech, I successfully completed projects like [mention a significant project], enhancing my problem-solving abilities and teamwork skills. I'm highly motivated, adaptable, and eager to learn, which will allow me to quickly contribute positively to your team."

*3. What are your strengths?*
Answer:
"My strengths include excellent problem-solving skills, strong analytical abilities, and effective communication. Throughout my academic projects and internships, I've demonstrated the ability to quickly learn new concepts, adapt to different situations, and work collaboratively within teams to deliver successful outcomes."

*4. What are your weaknesses?*
Answer:
"One area I'm currently improving upon is public speaking. Initially, speaking in front of large groups made me somewhat nervous. To overcome this, I've proactively participated in presentations, group discussions, and extracurricular activities to build my confidence. I've already noticed significant improvement, and I continue to work on this actively."

*5. Where do you see yourself in five years?*
Answer:
"In five years, I see myself in a position where I have significantly enhanced my technical and managerial skills, ideally progressing within your organization. I aim to take on increasing levels of responsibility and contribute to important projects, while also guiding newer team members, much like my mentors did for me."

*6. Describe a challenging situation you faced and how you handled it.*
Answer:
"During my final year project, our team faced a critical issue just a few days before submission. One component of our system malfunctioned unexpectedly. I took initiative, organized an emergency team meeting, reassigned roles based on individual strengths, and collaborated closely to troubleshoot. Through perseverance and teamwork, we resolved the issue efficiently and submitted our project successfully."
*7. What motivates you to do your best on the job?*
Answer:
"I'm motivated by opportunities to learn, tackle challenging problems, and contribute meaningfully to the team's success. Achieving goals and witnessing tangible results from my efforts further boosts my enthusiasm and commitment."

*8. Are you willing to relocate or travel for work?*
Answer:
"Yes, absolutely. I see relocation and travel as valuable opportunities to gain broader experience, learn new cultures, and further develop my professional skills. I'm flexible and open to exploring different locations to contribute effectively to the company's needs."

*9. Do you have any questions for us?*
Answer:
"Yes, thank you. Could you tell me about the initial responsibilities and expectations for this role? Also, what does success look like for someone in this position within their first six months?"

*10. How do you handle pressure and stress?*
Answer:
"I handle stress by staying organized and breaking tasks into smaller, manageable parts. During my B.Tech studies, especially during exams and projects, this approach helped me stay focused. Additionally, taking brief breaks to reflect and staying calm has consistently enabled me to deliver good results even under pressure."

*11. What is your greatest achievement so far?*
Answer:
"My greatest achievement was successfully leading our team in the final-year project titled [Project Name]. We won the best project award at our university exhibition. This experience not only boosted my technical skills but also developed my leadership and teamwork abilities."

*12. What do you know about our company?*
Answer:
"I've researched your company extensively and found that [Company Name] is well-known for innovation, high-quality products/services, and excellent industry reputation. Your recent project on [mention a notable recent project] particularly interests me, and I appreciate your commitment to employee development and corporate ethics."

*13. How do you see yourself contributing to our company?*
Answer:
"I intend to contribute by applying my knowledge in [mention specific skills related to your specialization], along with my adaptability and collaborative spirit. My project experiences and internships have equipped me with practical problem-solving skills which will allow me to add immediate value and support your team effectively."

*14. Describe your ideal workplace environment.*
Answer:
"My ideal workplace would be a collaborative and positive environment where creativity, innovation, and teamwork are highly valued. I appreciate a culture that encourages continuous learning, provides professional growth opportunities, and fosters open communication."

*15. Have you ever worked as part of a team? Describe your experience.*
Answer:
"Yes, I've actively participated in multiple team projects during my B.Tech. One notable instance was our mini-project on [mention a relevant topic]. Effective collaboration, clear communication, and mutual support were crucial to our project's success. This experience taught me the importance of team dynamics and achieving collective goals."

*16. Can you describe your leadership style?*
Answer:
"My leadership style is collaborative and inclusive. I believe in involving everyone‚Äôs ideas and making sure every member is heard. During my final year, I successfully led a team project by clearly communicating our goals, delegating responsibilities according to team members' strengths, and maintaining regular follow-ups to ensure everyone was on track."

*17. Are you comfortable working overtime or weekends if required?*
Answer:
"Yes, I understand that at times deadlines or special projects might require extra commitment. I'm flexible and willing to work overtime or weekends when necessary, understanding that teamwork and responsibility often require adapting to such situations."

*18. How do you keep yourself updated with technology and industry trends?*
Answer:
"I regularly follow technology blogs, attend webinars, and participate in online courses to keep myself updated. Platforms like LinkedIn, Coursera, and various technical forums help me stay informed about recent industry advancements and innovations."
*19. What salary expectations do you have as a fresher?*
Answer:
"As a fresher, my main focus is on gaining experience, professional growth, and contributing to the company's objectives. I trust your organization provides competitive remuneration, and I am confident that the offer would reflect industry standards for this role."

Proctoring & AI Monitoring

¬†
Test Rules & Structure

* The test contains multiple sections, each with a separate timer.

¬†
Coding & Submission Guidelines
* Sample code is provided ‚Äî please delete it and write your own.

* Ensure your output matches the exact format¬†mentioned in the problem statement.
* Use ‚ÄúRun‚Äù and ‚ÄúCustom Input‚Äù , any number of times, to test your code before submission.
* By clicking on Submit, your code will be auto-evaluated, and testcase-wise results will be displayed.
* You can submit each solution up to 5 times.
* Your last submitted version will be considered for scoring.
    * Failure to submit your solution will result in a Zero for that question.
¬†
Do‚Äôs & Don‚Äôts
Do‚Äôs:
* Close all background apps before starting (e.g., chat apps, browsers).
* Ensure your internet and camera are working.
Don‚Äôts:
* Do NOT switch tabs or navigate outside the test window.

There is no facility for safekeeping of your personal belongings outside the test hall and we are not responsible for any loss/theft. Only Admit Card, original Photo ID Card & Photo will be allowed inside the test hall.

4) Unfair Means: Adoption of any unfair means in the examination hall will result in disqualification from the TCS selection process.

5) Request for change of test centers wil NOT be entertained.

6) Friends and relatives accompanying the candidate will NOT be allowed inside the test centre.

*You will NOT be permitted to appear for the Exam if you fail to carry the Admit Card, photo and the mandatory Government issued Photo Identity Card.*

ÔøΩÔ∏è Before You Begin ‚Äî Essential Requirements
Before starting the test, you must complete the following:

2. Ensure your desktop/laptop has:
    * A functional webcam
    * Stable internet connection
    * Microphone in working condition

5. No calculators or other electronic devices may be used.
6. Do not browse, switch tabs, or open any external pages during the test.

‚è±Ô∏è Test Timing Rules (Strict Timer)
* The exam is controlled by a strict timer configuration.
* Test duration is fixed at 60 minutes.
* The form will automatically open and close at the scheduled time regardless of when you start.
* You must submit the form within the time window. Delayed submissions will NOT be accepted.

ÔøΩ Webcam Photo Capture
* Before the test begins, the system may capture your photo.
* You will be prompted for camera permission ‚Äî click ‚ÄúAllow‚Äù.
* If camera permission is denied, you will be unable to proceed.
* You may retake your photo or switch cameras (if available) before starting.

ÔøΩÔ∏è Full Screen Mode
* Once the test starts, your browser will be put into full-screen mode.
* You must stay in full screen until the test is submitted. 
* You can hide the message showing the full screen mode but don‚Äôt exit from full screen mode ‚Äì the exam will stop.
* The system will track and record any exits from full screen.

ÔøΩ Focus Tracking
* The test monitors if you switch tabs or applications.
* Tab switching, minimizing, or leaving the test windowwill be recorded. For such activity can cause the test to be terminated.
* Exiting full-screen or changing tabs may automatically terminate the test and your progress could be lost.

‚ùó Important Conduct Rules
* Do not switch tabs or open any links
* Do not browse or search externally
* Do not attempt to use unauthorized resources
* Any such activity may lead to termination of your test or disqualification.

ÔøΩ Form Submission
* The exam must be submitted within the time limit.
* If time expires, the system may auto-close and submission will not be accepted afterward.
* Ensure all questions are answered before submitting.
* Once the exam is submitted, you might need to exit from full screen mode or close the browser manually.

ÔøΩ Summary Checklist
Before starting:
* ‚òê Logged out of all email accounts
* ‚òê Using a desktop/laptop

*Do's & Dont's:*

- Assessment Content: The assessment will be a single assessment combining Java, Python, SQL skills. You can expect approximately 20-30 questions for 150 minutes. The questions will be a mix of   multiple-choice questions (MCQs), coding, short descriptive, and scenario-based questions.

- Proficiency Levels: This assessment will be at basic level.

- In-Person Requirement: You need to be available in person at the venue. Once attendance is marked, the test link will be shared via email.

- Test Link: The test link will be shared via email from Coderpad. Copy the link and open it in the Chrome browser. The link has two assessment tabs: Tutorial and Test. The Tutorial tab has 2-3 questions and is not mandatory; it is just to give you a feel of the portal.

- Screen Recording: Once the assessment starts, the associate‚Äôs screen is recorded by the Coderpad tool. Any switching windows/tabs or copy-pasting code will be reported as unusual activity, so please refrain from such activities which will lead to strong disciplinary actions. Taking a print screen will end your test.

- Submitting Answers: You need to submit every answer and then go to the next question. Your previously submitted answer can be changed at any point, provided you submit the changes again. The submit button is on the right side below every question.

- Ending the Test: Once the timer is over, the test will be auto submitted. However, if you complete the test before time, you need to end the test by going to the home tab (top left of the assessment screen) and selecting the end test option (top right of the home tab).

- Call Requirement: Until the assessment is completed, you need to be in front of the invigilator once done, you can leave by informing the invigilator that you have completed and submitted the test.
